| `fermionUpProjection_add_fermionDoublyProjection_eq_fermionUpNumber` / `fermionDownProjection_add_fermionDoublyProjection_eq_fermionDownNumber` / `fermionEmptyProjection_add_fermionUpProjection_eq_one_sub_fermionDownNumber` / `fermionEmptyProjection_add_fermionDownProjection_eq_one_sub_fermionUpNumber` | `p_тЖС+p_тЗИ = n_тЖС`; `p_тЖУ+p_тЗИ = n_тЖУ`; `p_тИЕ+p_тЖС = 1тИТn_тЖУ`; `p_тИЕ+p_тЖУ = 1тИТn_тЖС` (Hubbard per-site projection-aggregation: 4-state projections aggregate to spin-resolved number operators and complements) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SiteProjectionsSpinResolved.lean` (PR #1019) |
| (6 pairwise `Commute` lemmas) | `Commute (p_╬▒(i)) (p_╬▓(i))` for all 6 distinct `╬▒, ╬▓` тИИ `{тИЕ, тЖС, тЖУ, тЗИ}` (same-site Hubbard 4-state projections fully commute; trivial corollaries of PRs #1014, #1016, #1017, #1018 since both products vanish) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SiteProjectionsCommute.lean` (PR #1020) |
| `fermionDoublyProjection_pow_succ` / `fermionEmptyProjection_pow_succ` / `fermionUpProjection_pow_succ` / `fermionDownProjection_pow_succ` | `(p_╬▒(i))^(k+1) = p_╬▒(i)` for all 4 per-site projections (induction from PRs #1005, #1012; mirrors PR #992) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SiteProjectionsPow.lean` (PR #1034) |
| `fermionEmptyProjection_commute_of_any` | `Commute (p_тИЕ(i)) (p_тИЕ(j))` for any `i, j` (cross-site Hubbard empty projections commute; companion to PR #1006 for `p_тЗИ`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/EmptyProjectionCommute.lean` (PR #1035) |
| `fermionUpProjection_commute_of_any` / `fermionDownProjection_commute_of_any` | `Commute (p_тЖС(i)) (p_тЖС(j))`, `Commute (p_тЖУ(i)) (p_тЖУ(j))` for any `i, j` (cross-site Hubbard single-occupancy projections commute; completes diagonal cross-site Commute relations together with PRs #1006, #1035) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SingleProjectionsCommute.lean` (PR #1036) |
| `fermionUpProjection_commute_fermionDownProjection_of_any` | `Commute (p_тЖС(i)) (p_тЖУ(j))` for any `i, j` (cross-projection only-up vs only-down commute; non-diagonal extension) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/UpDownProjectionCommute.lean` (PR #1037) |
| (5 remaining cross-projection commutes) | `Commute (p_╬▒(i)) (p_╬▓(j))` for the 5 remaining `(╬▒, ╬▓)` pairs (PR #1038, completes the 16/16 cross-projection commute matrix together with PRs #1006, #1020, #1035, #1036, #1037) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/RemainingProjectionCommutes.lean` (PR #1038) |
| `hubbardAllDownState` / `fermionDownNumber_mulVec_allDownState` / `fermionUpNumber_mulVec_allDownState` / `hubbardOnSiteInteraction_mulVec_allDownState` / `fermionUpAnnihilation_mulVec_allDownState` / `fermionDownCreation_mulVec_allDownState` | all-down spin state for spinful Hubbard: `n_тЖУ┬╖|тЖУ..тЯй = |тЖУ..тЯй`, `n_тЖС┬╖|тЖУ..тЯй = 0`, `H_int┬╖|тЖУ..тЯй = 0`, etc. (mirror of `AllUpState.lean`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/AllDownState.lean` (PR #1039) |
| `fermionTotalDownNumber_mulVec_allDownState` / `fermionTotalUpNumber_mulVec_allDownState` / `fermionTotalSpinZ_mulVec_allDownState` / `fermionTotalSpinMinus_mulVec_allDownState` | `N_тЖУ┬╖|тЖУ..тЯй = (N+1)┬╖|тЖУ..тЯй`, `N_тЖС┬╖|тЖУ..тЯй = 0`, `S^z┬╖|тЖУ..тЯй = -(N+1)/2┬╖|тЖУ..тЯй` (lowest weight), `S^-┬╖|тЖУ..тЯй = 0` (mirror of `SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean`'s all-up versions) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/AllDownStateTotalNumber.lean` (PR #1040) |
| `fermionTotalSpinMinus_conjTranspose` / `fermionTotalSpinZ_isHermitian` / `fermionTotalSpinSquared_isHermitian` | `(┼Ь^-_tot)с┤┤ = ┼Ь^+_tot`; `(┼Ь^z_tot)` Hermitian; `(┼Ь┬▓_tot)` Hermitian (total-spin operator Hermiticity bundle) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinTotHermitian.lean` (PR #1041) |

### Multi-mode fermion via JordanтАУWigner (P2 backbone)

| Lean name | Statement | File |
|---|---|---|
| `jwString N i` | `тИП_{j.val < i.val} ╧Г^z_j` (noncomm-product, pairwise commutativity from `onSite_mul_onSite_of_ne`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `jwString_zero` | `jwString N 0 = 1` (empty product) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionMultiAnnihilation N i` | `c_i = jwString_i ┬╖ ╧Г^+_i` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionMultiCreation N i` | `c_iтАа = jwString_i ┬╖ ╧Г^-_i` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |

| `fermionMultiCreation_zero` | `c_0тАа = ╧Г^-_0` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `jwString_commute_onSite` | `Commute (jwString N i) (onSite i A)` (string commutes past same-site operators) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionMultiAnnihilation_sq` | `c_i┬▓ = 0` (Pauli exclusion) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionMultiCreation_sq` | `(c_iтАа)┬▓ = 0` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `jwString_isHermitian` | `(jwString N i)с┤┤ = jwString N i` (product of pairwise-commuting Hermitian ╧Г^z is Hermitian) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionMultiAnnihilation_conjTranspose` | `(c_i)с┤┤ = c_iтАа` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionMultiCreation_conjTranspose` | `(c_iтАа)с┤┤ = c_i` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `jwString_sq` | `(jwString N i)┬▓ = 1` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionMultiNumber N i` | `n_i := c_iтАа ┬╖ c_i` (site-occupation number operator) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |

| `fermionMultiNumber_isHermitian` | `n_i` is Hermitian | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionMultiNumber_sq` | `n_i┬▓ = n_i` (idempotent, eigenvalues 0, 1) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |

| `fermionMultiNumber_commute` | `Commute (n_i) (n_j)` for any sites (simultaneously diagonal) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |

| `fermionMultiAnnihilation_creation_anticomm_zero_one` | mixed: `c_0 ┬╖ c_1тАа + c_1тАа ┬╖ c_0 = 0` on `Fin (N+1)`, `N тЙе 1` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionMultiCreation_annihilation_anticomm_zero_one` | mixed dual: `c_0тАа ┬╖ c_1 + c_1 ┬╖ c_0тАа = 0` on `Fin (N+1)`, `N тЙе 1` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |

| `fermionMultiAnnihilation_anticomm_zero_pos` | **general cross-site CAR `{c_0, c_k} = 0`** for every `k : Fin (N+1)` with `0 < k.val` тАФ generalises the `_zero_one` / `_zero_two_general` specialisations. Proof: reduce to the anticommutator `{╧Г^+_0, jwString N k}`, which vanishes by induction on the string length (base: `{╧Г^+, ╧Г^z} = 0` at site 0; step: `╧Г^z_{k-1}` at site `k-1 тЙа 0` commutes past `╧Г^+_0`). | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |

| `fermionMultiCreation_annihilation_anticomm_zero_pos` | mixed dual `{c_0тАа, c_k} = 0` for every `k : Fin (N+1)` with `0 < k.val` (adjoint of the above) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |

| `fermionGenericHamiltonian_isHermitian` | `H = H_hop + V_int` is Hermitian when `t` is Hermitian and `V` is entry-wise real; one-line corollary of the two summand Hermiticities via `Matrix.IsHermitian.add` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |

| `fermionMultiVacuum N` | the JW vacuum on `Fin (N+1)` modes тАФ the all-up many-body basis vector `|тЖСтЖСтАжтЖСтЯй` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionMultiAnnihilation_mulVec_vacuum` | every annihilation operator kills the vacuum: `(c_i).mulVec (fermionMultiVacuum N) = 0` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionMultiNumber_mulVec_vacuum` | each `n_i ┬╖ |vacтЯй = 0` (since `n_i = c_iтАа c_i` and `c_i |vacтЯй = 0`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalNumber_mulVec_vacuum` | the vacuum is an `N╠В`-eigenstate of eigenvalue 0 | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionHopping_mulVec_vacuum` | `H_hop ┬╖ |vacтЯй = 0` (each `c_iтАа c_j |vacтЯй = c_iтАа 0 = 0`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionDensityInteraction_mulVec_vacuum` | `V_int ┬╖ |vacтЯй = 0` (each `n_i n_j |vacтЯй = n_i 0 = 0`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionGenericHamiltonian_mulVec_vacuum` | `H ┬╖ |vacтЯй = 0` for the full Hubbard skeleton (linearity) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalNumber_mulVec_singleParticle` | `c_iтАа |vacтЯй` is an `N╠В`-eigenstate of eigenvalue 1 (uses `[N╠В, c_iтАа] = c_iтАа` and `N╠В |vacтЯй = 0`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalNumber_mulVec_twoParticle` | `c_iтАа c_jтАа |vacтЯй` is an `N╠В`-eigenstate of eigenvalue 2 (Leibniz on the commutator gives `[N╠В, c_iтАа c_jтАа] = 2 c_iтАа c_jтАа`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalNumber_mulVec_eigenstate_of_commute` | generic charge-eigenstate helper: if `[N╠В, X] = ╬▒ X` and `N╠В v = 0` then `N╠В (X v) = ╬▒ (X v)`; abstracts the single- and two-particle constructions | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `spinfulIndex N i ╧Г` | bijection `(i, ╧Г : Fin 2) тЖж 2 * i + ╧Г тИИ Fin (2*N+2)`, embedding two-species data into a single-species JW chain | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionUpAnnihilation`, `fermionDownAnnihilation`, `fermionUpCreation`, `fermionDownCreation` | spinful annihilation / creation operators as wrappers around the underlying single-species operators at `2i` (up) and `2i+1` (down) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionUpNumber`, `fermionDownNumber` | spinful site-occupation numbers `n_{i,тЖС}`, `n_{i,тЖУ}` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardOnSiteInteraction N U` | the on-site Hubbard interaction `H_int = U ╬г_i n_{i,тЖС} ┬╖ n_{i,тЖУ}` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardOnSiteInteraction_commute_fermionTotalNumber` | `[H_int, N╠В] = 0` (charge conservation) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardOnSiteInteraction_isHermitian` | `H_int` is Hermitian when `U` is real (`star U = U`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardKinetic N t` | the spinful tight-binding kinetic operator `T = ╬г_{╧Г} ╬г_{i,j} t_{i,j} c_{i,╧Г}тАа c_{j,╧Г}` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardKinetic_commute_fermionTotalNumber` | `[T, N╠В] = 0` (charge conservation of the kinetic operator) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardKinetic_isHermitian` | `T` is Hermitian when `t` is a Hermitian matrix (`star (t i j) = t j i`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardHamiltonian N t U` | the canonical (single-band) Hubbard Hamiltonian `H = T + U ╬г n_{iтЖС} n_{iтЖУ}` on `Fin (2N+2)` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardHamiltonian_commute_fermionTotalNumber` | `[H, N╠В] = 0` (charge conservation) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardHamiltonian_isHermitian` | `H` is Hermitian when `t` is Hermitian and `U` is real | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardGibbsState N ╬▓ t U` | the Hubbard Gibbs state `gibbsState ╬▓ H_Hubbard` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardGibbsState_isHermitian` | Hermiticity (Hermitian `t`, real `U`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardGibbsState_commute_hamiltonian` | `Commute ╧Б_╬▓ H_Hubbard` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalUpNumber`, `fermionTotalDownNumber` | spinful conserved charges `N_тЖС = ╬г_i n_{iтЖС}`, `N_тЖУ = ╬г_i n_{iтЖУ}` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinZ` | total spin polarisation `S^z_tot = (1/2)(N_тЖС тИТ N_тЖУ)` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalUpNumber_commute_fermionTotalDownNumber` | `[N_тЖС, N_тЖУ] = 0` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalUpNumber_commute_fermionTotalNumber` / `fermionTotalDownNumber_commute_fermionTotalNumber` | `[N_тЖС, N╠В] = [N_тЖУ, N╠В] = 0` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinZ_commute_fermionTotalNumber` | `[S^z_tot, N╠В] = 0` (spin polarisation commutes with total number) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalUpNumber_commute_hubbardOnSiteInteraction` / `fermionTotalDownNumber_commute_hubbardOnSiteInteraction` | `[N_тЖС, H_int] = [N_тЖУ, H_int] = 0` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinZ_commute_hubbardOnSiteInteraction` | `[S^z_tot, H_int] = 0` (free corollary) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionUpAnnihilation_mulVec_vacuum` / `fermionDownAnnihilation_mulVec_vacuum` | every spinful annihilation kills the JW vacuum | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionUpNumber_mulVec_vacuum` / `fermionDownNumber_mulVec_vacuum` | each spinful site number kills the vacuum | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalUpNumber_mulVec_vacuum` / `fermionTotalDownNumber_mulVec_vacuum` | `N_тЖС ┬╖ |vacтЯй = N_тЖУ ┬╖ |vacтЯй = 0` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinZ_mulVec_vacuum` | `S^z_tot ┬╖ |vacтЯй = 0` (the vacuum is unpolarised) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardKinetic_mulVec_vacuum` / `hubbardOnSiteInteraction_mulVec_vacuum` / `hubbardHamiltonian_mulVec_vacuum` | each annihilates the vacuum (so `|vacтЯй` is a 0-energy / 0-particle eigenstate) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `spinfulIndex_up_ne_down` | the up-channel position `2 i` is never the down-channel position `2 j + 1` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalDownNumber_commute_fermionUp{Creation,Annihilation,Number}` and the dual `fermionTotalUpNumber_commute_fermionDown{Creation,Annihilation,Number}` | the spinful number on one species commutes with every operator of the other species (different JW positions) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `fermionTotalDownNumber_commute_upHopping` / `fermionTotalUpNumber_commute_downHopping` | the spinful same-╧Г hopping term `c_{i╧Г}тАа c_{j╧Г}` commutes with the opposite-spin total number `N_{╧Г'тЙа╧Г}` (cross-spin half of `[H_kinetic, N_╧Г] = 0`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |

#### Hubbard spin symmetry тАФ full SU(2) invariance (Tasaki ┬з9.3.3)

| Lean name | Statement | File |
|---|---|---|
| `fermionTotalUpNumber_isHermitian` / `fermionTotalDownNumber_isHermitian` | `N_тЖС` and `N_тЖУ` are Hermitian (sum of Hermitian number operators) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalUpNumber_commutator_fermionUpCreation` | `[N_тЖС, cтАа_{i,тЖС}] = cтАа_{i,тЖС}` (up-spin sub-chain analogue of `[N╠В, cтАа_i] = cтАа_i`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalDownNumber_commutator_fermionDownCreation` | `[N_тЖУ, cтАа_{i,тЖУ}] = cтАа_{i,тЖУ}` | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalUpNumber_commute_upHopping` | `[N_тЖС, cтАа_{i,тЖС} c_{j,тЖС}] = 0` (same-species hopping preserves spin-up count) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalDownNumber_commute_downHopping` | `[N_тЖУ, cтАа_{i,тЖУ} c_{j,тЖУ}] = 0` | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalUpNumber_commute_hubbardKinetic` / `fermionTotalDownNumber_commute_hubbardKinetic` | `[N_тЖС, H_kin] = [N_тЖУ, H_kin] = 0` (each spin species conserved by kinetic term) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalUpNumber_commute_hubbardHamiltonian` | `[N_тЖС, H] = 0` (Tasaki ┬з9.3.3, eq. (9.3.35)) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalDownNumber_commute_hubbardHamiltonian` | `[N_тЖУ, H] = 0` (Tasaki ┬з9.3.3, eq. (9.3.35)) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinZ_commute_hubbardHamiltonian` | `[S^z_tot, H] = 0` (Tasaki ┬з9.3.3, p. 333) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinPlus` / `fermionTotalSpinMinus` | `┼Ь^+_tot = ╬г_i cтАа_{i,тЖС}c_{i,тЖУ}`, `┼Ь^-_tot = (┼Ь^+_tot)тАа` тАФ SU(2) raising/lowering operators (Tasaki ┬з9.3.3, p. 332) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinPlus_conjTranspose` | `(┼Ь^+_tot)тАа = ┼Ь^-_tot` | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionUpAnnihilation_commutator_fermionTotalSpinPlus` | `[c_{j,тЖС}, ┼Ь^+_tot] = c_{j,тЖУ}` (Tasaki ┬з9.3.3, eq. (9.3.36)) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionDownCreation_commutator_fermionTotalSpinPlus` | `[cтАа_{j,тЖУ}, ┼Ь^+_tot] = тИТcтАа_{j,тЖС}` (Tasaki ┬з9.3.3, eq. (9.3.36)) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionUpCreation_commute_fermionTotalSpinPlus` / `fermionDownAnnihilation_commute_fermionTotalSpinPlus` | `[cтАа_{i,тЖС}, ┼Ь^+_tot] = 0` and `[c_{j,тЖУ}, ┼Ь^+_tot] = 0` (Tasaki ┬з9.3.3, eq. (9.3.36)) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinPlus_commute_hubbardHamiltonian` | `[┼Ь^+_tot, H] = 0` (Tasaki ┬з9.3.3, eq. (9.3.35)) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinMinus_commute_hubbardHamiltonian` | `[┼Ь^-_tot, H] = 0` (Tasaki ┬з9.3.3, eq. (9.3.35), proved by adjoint) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SpinSymmetry.lean` |

#### Hubbard all-up-spin state and saturated ferromagnetism (Tasaki ┬з11.1.1)

| Lean name | Statement | File |
|---|---|---|
| `hubbardAllUpState N` | fully spin-polarised basis vector: all spin-up orbitals occupied, spin-down empty (even JW indices = 1, odd = 0) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/AllUpState.lean` |
| `fermionUpNumber_mulVec_allUpState` | `n_{i,тЖС} ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй` тАФ each spin-up number operator acts as identity on the all-up state | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/AllUpState.lean` |
| `fermionDownNumber_mulVec_allUpState` | `n_{i,тЖУ} ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = 0` тАФ no spin-down electrons; key to the vanishing of `H_int` | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/AllUpState.lean` |
| `hubbardOnSiteInteraction_mulVec_allUpState` | `H_int ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = 0` тАФ no double occupancy in the fully-polarised state (Tasaki ┬з11.1.1, p. 373; eq. (10.1.5), p. 344) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/AllUpState.lean` |
| `hubbardHamiltonian_mulVec_allUpState` | `H ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = H_hop ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй` тАФ the Hubbard model in the all-up sector reduces to a non-interacting hopping problem | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/AllUpState.lean` |
| `fermionDownAnnihilation_mulVec_allUpState` | `c_{i,тЖУ} ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = 0` тАФ spin-down annihilation kills the all-up state (odd JW index unoccupied, so ╧ГтБ║ maps it to 0) (Tasaki ┬з11.1.1, p. 373) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/AllUpState.lean` |
| `fermionUpCreation_mulVec_allUpState` | `cтАа_{i,тЖС} ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = 0` тАФ spin-up creation kills the all-up state (even JW index already occupied, so ╧ГтБ╗ maps it to 0) (Tasaki ┬з11.1.1, p. 373) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/AllUpState.lean` |
| `hubbardKinetic_mulVec_allUpState` | `H_hop ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = (╬г_i t i i) тАв |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй` тАФ hopping eigenvalue: off-diagonal terms vanish by CAR anticommutation, diagonal terms give 1 each (Tasaki ┬з11.1.1, p. 373) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/AllUpState.lean` |
| `hubbardHamiltonian_mulVec_allUpState_eigenstate` | `H ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = (╬г_i t i i) тАв |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй` тАФ full Hamiltonian eigenstate: combines `H_hop` eigenvalue and `H_int ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = 0` (Tasaki ┬з11.1.1, p. 373; eq. (10.1.5), p. 344) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/AllUpState.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinSquared` | total-spin Casimir `(┼Ь_tot)┬▓ = ┼ЬтБ╗┼ЬтБ║ + ┼Ь_z(┼Ь_z+1)` | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean` |
| `fermionTotalUpNumber_mulVec_allUpState` | `N_тЖС ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = (N+1) тАв |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй` | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean` |
| `fermionTotalDownNumber_mulVec_allUpState` | `N_тЖУ ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = 0` | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinZ_mulVec_allUpState` | `┼Ь^z_tot ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = ((N+1)/2) тАв |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй` | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinPlus_mulVec_allUpState` | `┼ЬтБ║_tot ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = 0` тАФ highest-weight state; no down-spin to raise | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinSquared_mulVec_allUpState` | `(┼Ь_tot)┬▓ ┬╖ |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй = S_max(S_max+1) тАв |тЖСтАжтЖСтЯй` where `S_max = (N+1)/2` (Tasaki ┬з11.1.1, p. 372) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinSquared_commute_hubbardHamiltonian` | `[(┼Ь_tot)┬▓, H] = 0` тАФ Casimir commutes with H (from SU(2) invariance, Tasaki ┬з9.3.3) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean` |
| `isSaturatedFerromagnet` | **Definition 11.1** тАФ Lean predicate: there exists a ground-state energy `EтВА` such that every nonzero `H`-eigenvector with eigenvalue `EтВА` is a `(┼Ь_tot)┬▓`-eigenvector with eigenvalue `S_max(S_max+1)` (Tasaki ┬з11.1.1, p. 372) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinZ_commutator_fermionTotalSpinMinus` | `[┼Ь^z_tot, ┼Ь^-_tot] = -┼Ь^-_tot` тАФ SU(2) algebra relation; follows from site-wise `[┼Ь_z, cтАа_{i,тЖУ}c_{i,тЖС}] = -(cтАа_{i,тЖУ}c_{i,тЖС})` (Tasaki ┬з9.3.3, p. 332) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinMinus_mulVec_preserves_hamiltonian_eigenvalue` | if `H┬╖v = E┬╖v` then `H┬╖(┼Ь^-┬╖v) = E┬╖(┼Ь^-┬╖v)` тАФ applying `┼Ь^-` preserves Hamiltonian eigenvalues; follows from `[┼Ь^-, H] = 0` (Tasaki ┬з11.1.1, p. 373) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean` |
| `fermionTotalSpinZ_mulVec_spinMinus_step` | if `┼Ь_z┬╖v = m┬╖v` then `┼Ь_z┬╖(┼Ь^-┬╖v) = (m-1)┬╖(┼Ь^-┬╖v)` тАФ applying `┼Ь^-` decrements `┼Ь_z` eigenvalue by 1; follows from `[┼Ь^z, ┼Ь^-] = -┼Ь^-` (Tasaki ┬з2.4, eq. (2.4.9); ┬з11.1.1, p. 373) | `Fermion/JordanWigner/Hubbard/SaturatedFerromagnetism.lean` |

| `hubbardKineticOnGraph N G J` | spinful Hubbard kinetic operator from a `SimpleGraph G` and edge weight `J` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardKineticOnGraph_commute_fermionTotalNumber` / `hubbardKineticOnGraph_isHermitian` | charge conservation always; Hermiticity for real `J` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardHamiltonianOnGraph N G J U` | full Hubbard Hamiltonian from a graph + on-site coupling | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardHamiltonianOnGraph_commute_fermionTotalNumber` / `hubbardHamiltonianOnGraph_isHermitian` | charge conservation; Hermiticity for real `J` and real `U` | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardChainHamiltonian N J U` | the canonical 1D nearest-neighbour Hubbard chain `тИТJ ╬г_{╧Г,тЯиi,jтЯй} c_{i╧Г}тАа c_{j╧Г} + U ╬г_i n_{iтЖС} n_{iтЖУ}` (built from `pathGraph (N+1)`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardChainHamiltonian_isHermitian` / `hubbardChainHamiltonian_commute_fermionTotalNumber` | Hermiticity (real `J, U`) and charge conservation | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardHamiltonianOnGraph_mulVec_vacuum` / `hubbardChainHamiltonian_mulVec_vacuum` | both graph-built Hubbard Hamiltonians annihilate the JW vacuum | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardChainGibbsState N ╬▓ J U` | Gibbs state of the 1D Hubbard chain | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardChainGibbsState_isHermitian` / `hubbardChainGibbsState_commute_hamiltonian` | Hermiticity (real `J, U`) and commute with the Hamiltonian | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardCycleGibbsState_commute_hamiltonian` | the periodic Hubbard Gibbs state commutes with the periodic Hubbard Hamiltonian (companion of the open-chain version, free corollary of `gibbsState_commute_hamiltonian`) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardChainGibbsExpectation_zero` / `_im_of_isHermitian` / `_commutator_hamiltonian` / `_hamiltonian_im` / `_hamiltonian_pow_im` / `hubbardChain_partitionFn_im` / `_ofReal_re_eq` / `hubbardChainGibbsState_pow_trace` | open-chain Hubbard expectation companions (╬▓ = 0 closed form, Hermitian-observable real, conservation, energy / energy-power expectations real, partition function real, real-cast, R├йnyi-n trace) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |
| `hubbardCycleGibbsExpectation_zero` / `_im_of_isHermitian` / `_commutator_hamiltonian` / `_hamiltonian_im` / `_hamiltonian_pow_im` / `hubbardCycle_partitionFn_im` / `_ofReal_re_eq` / `hubbardCycleGibbsState_pow_trace` | periodic Hubbard chain expectation companions (same family as the open chain) | `Fermion/JordanWigner.lean` |

## Continuum-limit roadmap

The project's long-term goals include the `╧Ж^4` / Ising continuum
limit and lattice-QCD-style formalisations, both of which are defined
as limits `a тЖТ 0` of families of finite-spacing lattice systems. A
survey of the gap between the current finite-volume matrix framework
and what the continuum limit actually demands was recorded during
Phase A scoping (consulted codex twice on scope and design choices)
and proposes the four phases below.

**Phase A (current, this PR)**. Add a **thin type-level tag**
`class LatticeWithSpacing (╬Ы : Type*) where spacing : тДЭтЙе0`
so that a lattice spacing `a : тДЭтЙе0` can be attached to `╬Ы` as
metadata. Provide the default instance `Fin (N + 1)` with
`spacing := 1` so every pre-existing Hamiltonian in the library is
`rfl`-equivalent to its `spacing := 1` specialisation. No geometry,
no rescaling, no continuum object.

**Phase B (deferred)**. Lattice sequences `╬Ы_n` with
`spacing a_n тЖТ 0`, rescaling of coupling constants
(`J_n = ─е ┬╖ a_n^{-2+d}` etc.), and lattice-point embeddings in
`тДЭ^d`. Introduce when a concrete theorem (e.g. Osterwalder-Schrader,
a specific block-spin transformation) requires iterating over a
spacing sequence.

**Phase C (deferred)**. Operator-valued distribution / GNS /
Hilbert-space infrastructure to house the continuum limit itself.
Per codex (2026-04-22), we do **not** generalise
`ManyBodyOp ╬Ы = Matrix _ _ тДВ` to a type class preemptively: existing
proofs depend on Matrix-specific API (`conjTranspose`, `exp`,
`trace`, `mulVec`, entry formulas), and the right abstraction becomes
clear only once a second concrete backend (infinite-volume Hilbert
space, quasi-local C*-algebra) is in place.

**Phase D (deferred)**. Coupling-constant running
`g : тДЭтЙе0 тЖТ тДЭ` and renormalisation-group transformations. Follows
phases B-C.

| Lean name | Statement | File |
|---|---|---|
| `LatticeWithSpacing` | `class LatticeWithSpacing (╬Ы : Type*) where spacing : тДЭтЙе0` тАФ thin type-level tag recording the lattice spacing `a : тДЭтЙе0` of a vertex type | `Lattice/Scale.lean` |
| `spacingOf` | `spacingOf ╬Ы := LatticeWithSpacing.spacing` тАФ named accessor | `Lattice/Scale.lean` |
| `instLatticeWithSpacingFinSucc` | default `spacing := 1` instance for `Fin (N + 1)`, making every existing Hamiltonian `rfl`-equivalent to the unit-spacing specialisation | `Lattice/Scale.lean` |
| `spacing_fin_succ` / `spacingOf_fin_succ` | `spacing = 1` computed at `Fin (N + 1)` | `Lattice/Scale.lean` |
| `instLatticeWithSpacingInt` | default `spacing := 1` instance for `тДд` (infinite chain тАФ matches `integerChainGraph`) | `Lattice/Scale.lean` |
| `instLatticeWithSpacingIntSq` | default `spacing := 1` instance for `тДд ├Ч тДд` (infinite 2D square lattice тАФ matches `integerSquareLatticeGraph`) | `Lattice/Scale.lean` |
| `spacing_int` / `spacingOf_int` / `spacing_int_sq` / `spacingOf_int_sq` | `spacing = 1` computed at `тДд`, `тДд ├Ч тДд` | `Lattice/Scale.lean` |

## Open items / axioms

The following Tasaki ┬з2.1 / ┬з2.2 items are **not yet fully proved**.
They are tracked here so that future PRs can pick them up and replace
each axiom by a proof (or fill in the deferred construction).

### ~~TODO (P1d''') тАФ Problem 2.1.a for general `S тЙе 1`~~ **DONE**

**Statement (Tasaki p.15)**: For any spin `S`, every operator on the
single-site Hilbert space `h_0 = тДВ^{2S+1}` (i.e. every `(2S+1) ├Ч (2S+1)`
matrix) can be written as a polynomial in `1╠В, ┼Ь^(1), ┼Ь^(2), ┼Ь^(3)`.

**Status**: Done in general spin-`S` form (Issue #458 closed in PR #490).
The headline theorem `LatticeSystem.Quantum.spinS_adjoin_eq_top` proves

```
Algebra.adjoin тДВ {┼Ь^(1) N, ┼Ь^(2) N, ┼Ь^(3) N}
  = (тКд : Subalgebra тДВ (Matrix (Fin (N+1)) (Fin (N+1)) тДВ))
```

via Tasaki solution S.1: diagonal projectors `P_k` are Lagrange-interpolation
polynomials in `┼Ь^{(3)}` (`spinSDiagProj_eq_lagrange_aeval`); off-diagonal
matrix units `E_{i,j}` are products of ladder-step units
(`single_offset_succ_{,swap_}mem_adjoin`); the entry-wise decomposition
`M = тИС_{i,j} M_{i,j} тАв E_{i,j}` then closes the spanning. The earlier
concrete-case modules `pauliBasis` (`S = 1/2`) and `spinOne_decomposition`
(`S = 1`) remain as illustrative specialisations.

### ~~TODO тАФ Tasaki Problem 2.2.c (SU(2) non-invariance / averaged state)~~ **DONE**

**Statement (Tasaki p.23, eq. (2.2.15))**: An explicit averaged state
of the form

```
(1/4╧А) тИлтВА^{2╧А} d╧Ж тИлтВА^╧А d╬╕ sin ╬╕ ┬╖ ├Ы^(3)_╧Ж ┬╖ ├Ы^(2)_╬╕ ┬╖ |тЖСтВБтЯй|тЖУтВВтЯй
```

equals (up to phase) the singlet `(1/тИЪ2)(|тЖСтВБтЯй|тЖУтВВтЯй - |тЖУтВБтЯй|тЖСтВВтЯй)`. The
problem asks to verify this and to characterize states that fail to be
SU(2)-invariant.

**Status**: Formally proved with zero `sorry` in `Quantum/SU2Integral.lean`
as `problem_2_2_c`. The proof integrates over the Euler-angle parameter space
using `integral_cexp_I_mul_zero_two_pi`, `integral_cexp_neg_I_mul_zero_two_pi`,
and the half-angle trig integrals established in earlier PRs. See
`Quantum/SpinHalfRotation.lean` for `spinHalfRot3_mul_spinHalfRot2_mulVec_spinHalfDown`
and `Quantum/SU2Integral.lean` for all supporting lemmas.

### TODO тАФ Tasaki ┬з2.5 antiferromagnetic deferred items (issue [#240](https://github.com/phasetr/lattice-system/issues/240))

The antiferromagnetic Heisenberg / N├йel state machinery in
Tasaki ┬з2.5 is largely formalised (chain / 2D / 3D N├йel states +
per-bond expectations `-1/4` + generic graph-centric `neelStateOf`
+ Marshall sign machinery + time-reversal action; see Roadmap row
P1k above). The following subitems remain deferred (large
mathematical work):

- **Marshall-Lieb-Mattis Theorem 2.2** (uniqueness + sign
  structure of the AFM ground state). Requires a Perron-Frobenius
  argument on the Marshall-rotated basis.
- **Problem 2.5.a** (single-cluster ground-state energy
  `-S(1+zS)` for general spin `S` and coordination `z`).
  Requires general-spin infrastructure (P1d''' above is now done in PR #490; this remains for the ┬з2.5-specific cluster argument).
- **Problem 2.5.b** (lower bound on `E_GS` via 2.5.a).
- **Problem 2.5.c** (single-site expectation `тЯи┼Ь_xтЯй = 0` in the
  AFM ground state).
- **Problem 2.5.d** (two-spin correlation under MLM).

The generic graph-centric `neelStateOf` (Phase 3 PR #331) is the
foundation on which these will be built when general-spin and
Perron-Frobenius infrastructure becomes available.

### TODO тАФ remove remaining 7 per-theorem linter suppressions (issue [#377](https://github.com/phasetr/lattice-system/issues/377))

Phase 4 substantially closed `lake build` warnings (zero warnings
+ zero errors as of 2026-04-23), with the exception of 7
per-theorem `set_option linter.{flexible,unusedTactic,unusedSimpArgs} false in`
blocks (4 in `SpinOne{Basis,Decomp}`, 3 in
`SpinHalfRotation/Conjugation`). All are comment-justified and
listed in the [Deprecation window](deprecations.html#remaining-linter-suppressions)
page. Removal requires interactive `simp?` per sub-case.

## Links

- API documentation (doc-gen4): **currently disabled** тАФ the
  CI job was consistently slow (often >1h). To build the API docs
  locally, run
  `lake build +Mathlib:docs` or consult the
  [doc-gen4 README](https://github.com/leanprover-community/doc-gen4).
  The CI job is commented out in
  `.github/workflows/lean_action_ci.yml` with a note on how to
  re-enable.
